<div class="gb-grid-column gb-grid-column-2184e42b"><div class="gb-container gb-container-2184e42b">

<p style="font-size:19px">Just because you&#8217;re in your golden years doesn&#8217;t mean you can&#8217;t play the best golf of your life. Founded by Erin Blakely, a golfer, licensed nursing home administrator, and geriatric social worker, she combines her passion for golf with her knowledge of healthy aging. </p>



<p style="font-size:19px">Since 2022, Senior Golf Source has grown into a team of golf experts and senior testers with over 150+ years of combined experience.</p>



<p style="font-size:19px">Our mission at Senior Golf Source is to be the preferred online community for over 50 players seeking expert advice and content specifically tested by senior golfers. </p>

</div></div>
</div>
